# Bandit

For dead NPCs named "Bandit", see [Bandit (dead)](Skyrim_Bandit_(dead).md). For other uses, see [Bandit (disambiguation)](Skyrim_Bandit_(disambiguation).md).

[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/a/ac/SR-npc-Bandit_27.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_27.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_27.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_27.jpg) Bandits **Bandits** are rogue lawbreakers living a life of plunder and are one of the most common enemy types in [Skyrim](Skyrim_Skyrim.md). You will typically find them in camps, some of which are [marked](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps) on your map, and some of which are [unmarked](Skyrim_Unmarked_Places.md#Unmarked_Bandit_and_Forsworn_Camps). Of the marked locations, bandits often inhabit both the interiors and exteriors of fort-type and other structures.

Although most bandits will attack you on sight, some may attack only when you get too close. Still others will demand that you pay them and attack if you refuse. Bandits can be members of any race (except [Altmer](Skyrim_High_Elf.md)), and may be spellcasters, archers, one-handed melee fighters, or two-handed melee fighters.

## Bandit Types
While the stronger bandit types will not appear until after you've reached the levels shown, you will continue to meet low-level versions even at high levels. Boss-level bandits will always be at the highest possible level, and will normally be identified as "Bandit Chief". Bandits of each type may vary in the combat equipment and style they use.

Normal Bandits are generally fairly easy to kill, while Bandit Chiefs and Marauders are tougher. Unlike other Bandit Marauders, Bandit Marauder mages (bandits with the [Bandit Wizard](Skyrim_Bandit_Wizard.md) class) begin appearing at level 24.

![](https://images.uesp.net/8/8a/Skyrim-Box-TL.gif)

![](https://images.uesp.net/f/f4/Skyrim-Box-TR.gif)

![](https://images.uesp.net/6/60/Skyrim-Box-BL.gif)

![](https://images.uesp.net/9/99/Skyrim-Box-BR.gif)

### One-Handed Melee
These bandits wield one-handed melee weapons and shields in battle. They carry one of the following weapons, depending on your level:

- **Mace:** [iron mace](Skyrim_Iron_Mace.md), [steel mace](Skyrim_Steel_Mace.md), [Orcish mace](Skyrim_Orcish_Mace.md), [Dwarven mace](Skyrim_Dwarven_Mace.md), [Elven mace](Skyrim_Elven_Mace.md) or [Nordic mace](Skyrim_Nordic_Mace.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Sword:** [iron sword](Skyrim_Iron_Sword.md), [steel sword](Skyrim_Steel_Sword.md), [orcish sword](Skyrim_Orcish_Sword.md), [Dwarven sword](Skyrim_Dwarven_Sword.md), [Elven sword](Skyrim_Elven_Sword.md) or [Nordic sword](Skyrim_Nordic_Sword.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **War Axe:** [iron war axe](Skyrim_Iron_War_Axe.md), [steel war axe](Skyrim_Steel_War_Axe.md), [Orcish war axe](Skyrim_Orcish_War_Axe.md), [Dwarven war axe](Skyrim_Dwarven_War_Axe.md), [Elven war axe](Skyrim_Elven_War_Axe.md) or [Nordic war axe](Skyrim_Nordic_War_Axe.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>

All bandits also carry a random assortment of items, which include [beverages](Skyrim_Food.md#Beverages), [lockpicks](Skyrim_Lockpick.md), [food](Skyrim_Food.md), [jewelry](Skyrim_Jewelry.md), [gems](Skyrim_Gems.md), tools, [ingots](Skyrim_Ingots.md), and a small amount of gold. Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry more gold and may carry additional lockpicks.

#### Light Armor
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/f/f5/SR-npc-Bandit_06.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_06.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_06.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_06.jpg) A Bandit Marauder looking for trouble In addition to the weapons listed above, these bandits wear a set of leveled light armor:

- **Cuirass:** [fur armor](Skyrim_Fur_Armor.md), [hide armor](Skyrim_Hide_Armor.md), [studded armor](Skyrim_Studded_Armor.md), [leather armor](Skyrim_Leather_Armor.md), [scaled armor](Skyrim_Scaled_Armor.md), or [scaled horn armor](Skyrim_Scaled_Horn_Armor.md)
- **Boots:** [fur shoes](Skyrim_Fur_Shoes.md), [hide boots](Skyrim_Hide_Boots.md), [leather boots](Skyrim_Leather_Boots.md), or [scaled boots](Skyrim_Scaled_Boots.md)
- **Gauntlets:** 50% chance of [fur bracers](Skyrim_Fur_Bracers.md), [hide bracers](Skyrim_Hide_Bracers.md), [leather bracers](Skyrim_Leather_Bracers.md), or [scaled bracers](Skyrim_Scaled_Bracers.md)
- **Shield:** 20% chance of a [hide shield](Skyrim_Hide_Shield.md), [iron shield](Skyrim_Iron_Shield.md), or [elven shield](Skyrim_Elven_Shield.md)

[^1](#note_Not Archer) This male Redguard bandit (`Enc Bandit01Melee1HRedguard M`) also appears in the list of level 1 archers (`Sub Char Bandit01Missile`), but has all the stats and inventory appropriate for a one-handed weapon fighter. [^2](#note_Level0) These Bandit Highwaymen are actually set as level 0; they have lower health and stamina than other bandits that appear when you are the appropriate level. If [Dragonborn](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md) is installed, their level and stats will be corrected (hover to see values).
#### Heavy Armor
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/2/2f/SR-npc-Bandit_15.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_15.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_15.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_15.jpg) A Bandit Thug in full steel armor These bandits wield one-handed melee weapons and shields in battle. They carry the same weapons and miscellaneous items as their light armor counterparts, and wear a set of leveled heavy armor:

- **Cuirass:** [iron armor](Skyrim_Iron_Armor.md), [steel armor](Skyrim_Steel_Armor.md), [steel plate armor](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Armor.md), or [Nordic carved armor](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Armor.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Boots:** [iron boots](Skyrim_Iron_Boots.md), [steel cuffed boots](Skyrim_Steel_Cuffed_Boots.md), [steel plate boots](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Boots.md), or [Nordic carved boots](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Boots.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Gauntlets:** 50% chance of [iron gauntlets](Skyrim_Iron_Gauntlets.md), [steel Nordic gauntlets](Skyrim_Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets.md), [steel Imperial gauntlets](Skyrim_Steel_Imperial_Gauntlets.md), [steel plate gauntlets](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Gauntlets.md), or [Nordic carved gauntlets](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Gauntlets.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Helmet:** [iron helmet](Skyrim_Iron_Helmet.md), [steel helmet](Skyrim_Steel_Helmet.md), [steel horned helmet](Skyrim_Steel_Horned_Helmet.md), [steel plate helmet](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Helmet.md), or [Nordic carved helmet](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Helmet.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Shield:** [hide shield](Skyrim_Hide_Shield.md), [iron shield](Skyrim_Iron_Shield.md), [banded iron shield](Skyrim_Banded_Iron_Shield.md), or [steel shield](Skyrim_Steel_Shield.md)

### Two-Handed Melee
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/3/32/SR-npc-Bandit_07.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_07.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_07.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_07.jpg) A Bandit fighter wielding his fearsome greatsword These bandits carry large, two-handed melee weapons into the fray. They wear the same leveled armor as their one-handed light armored counterparts (without the shield), and also carry one of the following weapons, depending on your level:

- **Battleaxe:** [iron battleaxe](Skyrim_Iron_Battleaxe.md), [steel battleaxe](Skyrim_Steel_Battleaxe.md), [Orcish battleaxe](Skyrim_Orcish_Battleaxe.md), [Dwarven battleaxe](Skyrim_Dwarven_Battleaxe.md), [Elven battleaxe](Skyrim_Elven_Battleaxe.md) or [Nordic battleaxe](Skyrim_Nordic_Battleaxe.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Greatsword:** [iron greatsword](Skyrim_Iron_Greatsword.md), [steel greatsword](Skyrim_Steel_Greatsword.md), [Orcish greatsword](Skyrim_Orcish_Greatsword.md), [Dwarven greatsword](Skyrim_Dwarven_Greatsword.md), [Elven greatsword](Skyrim_Elven_Greatsword.md) or [Nordic greatsword](Skyrim_Nordic_Greatsword.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Warhammer:** [iron warhammer](Skyrim_Iron_Warhammer.md), [steel warhammer](Skyrim_Steel_Warhammer.md), [Orcish warhammer](Skyrim_Orcish_Warhammer.md), [Dwarven warhammer](Skyrim_Dwarven_Warhammer.md), [Elven warhammer](Skyrim_Elven_Warhammer.md) or [Nordic warhammer](Skyrim_Nordic_Warhammer.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>

Two-handed melee bandits also carry a small amount of gold and have a chance to carry a few lockpicks. Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry an [orcish dagger](Skyrim_Orcish_Dagger.md) and have no lockpicks.

[^1](#note_Berserker) These two-handed melee bandits appear in "berserker" leveled lists; they are identical to other two-handed fighters, except that they have a morality of `No Crime` instead of `Any Crime` and have the `cs Human Berserker Lvl1` fighting style instead of `cs Human Melee Lvl1`. - ![PC Only](https://images.uesp.net/d/d7/Computer.svg)
The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch) fixes this bug.

[^2](#note_Also Level5) `Sub Char Bandit01Melee2HBerserk` and `Sub Char Bandit02Melee2HBerserk` contain the same list of bandits, which means the berserkers that appear in the level 1 list also appear in the level 5 list (with stats and perks appropriate for level 1 bandits). - ![PC Only](https://images.uesp.net/d/d7/Computer.svg)
The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.

### Archers
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/3/3e/SR-npc-Bandit_24.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_24.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_24.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_24.jpg) A Bandit Marauder drawing a deadly arrow Archer bandits prefer to keep their distance, using a bow and arrows to attack. These bandits have the [Bandit Archer](Skyrim_Bandit_Archer.md) class. They wear the same leveled armor as [melee bandits](#One-Handed_Melee), and also one of each of the following weapon types, depending on your level:

- **Bow:** [long bow](Skyrim_Long_Bow.md), [hunting bow](Skyrim_Hunting_Bow.md), [Imperial bow](Skyrim_Imperial_Bow.md), [Orcish bow](Skyrim_Orcish_Bow.md), [Dwarven bow](Skyrim_Dwarven_Bow.md), [Elven bow](Skyrim_Elven_Bow.md) or [Nordic bow](Skyrim_Nordic_Bow.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Arrows (20):** [iron arrow](Skyrim_Iron_Arrow.md), [steel arrow](Skyrim_Steel_Arrow.md), [Orcish arrow](Skyrim_Orcish_Arrow.md), [Dwarven arrow](Skyrim_Dwarven_Arrow.md), [Elven arrow](Skyrim_Elven_Arrow.md) or [Nordic arrow](Skyrim_Nordic_Arrow.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Dagger:** [iron dagger](Skyrim_Iron_Dagger.md), [steel dagger](Skyrim_Steel_Dagger.md), [Orcish dagger](Skyrim_Orcish_Dagger.md), [Dwarven dagger](Skyrim_Dwarven_Dagger.md), [Elven dagger](Skyrim_Elven_Dagger.md) or [Nordic dagger](Skyrim_Nordic_Dagger.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>

Archers carry the same miscellaneous loot as their one-handed counterparts, and also have a small chance of carrying additional arrows of any type (including [glass](Skyrim_Glass_Arrow.md), [ebony](Skyrim_Ebony_Arrow.md), and [Daedric](Skyrim_Daedric_Arrow.md)). Archer Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry more gold than those at lower levels.

[^1](#note_Not Archer2) This male Redguard bandit (`Enc Bandit01Melee1HRedguard M`) has all the stats and inventory appropriate for a one-handed weapon fighter, and also appears in the list of level 1 one-handed melee bandits (`Sub Char Bandit01Melee1H`). [^2](#note_Cat) None of the Khajiit archers can actually appear in-game as they never got added to the respective leveled list. - ![PC Only](https://images.uesp.net/d/d7/Computer.svg)
The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.

### Mages
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/b/b6/SR-npc-Bandit_25.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_25.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_25.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_25.jpg) A bandit mage dual-wielding shock spells Bandit mages rely primarily on spellcasting in battle. They wear the following leveled armor:

- **Cuirass:** [fur armor](Skyrim_Fur_Armor.md)
- **Boots:** [fur shoes](Skyrim_Fur_Shoes.md), [hide boots](Skyrim_Hide_Boots.md), [leather boots](Skyrim_Leather_Boots.md), or [scaled boots](Skyrim_Scaled_Boots.md)

Bandit and Bandit Outlaw mages carry an [iron dagger](Skyrim_Iron_Dagger.md), while Bandit Thug mages carry a [steel dagger](Skyrim_Steel_Dagger.md). Bandit Highwayman, Bandit Plunderer, and Bandit Marauder mages carry a leveled dagger ([iron](Skyrim_Iron_Dagger.md), [steel](Skyrim_Steel_Dagger.md), [orcish](Skyrim_Orcish_Dagger.md), [dwarven](Skyrim_Dwarven_Dagger.md), or [elven](Skyrim_Elven_Dagger.md)).

In addition to their gear, bandit mages carry a random assortment of items, including [lockpicks](Skyrim_Lockpick.md), [food](Skyrim_Food.md), [jewelry](Skyrim_Jewelry.md), [soul gems](Skyrim_Soul_Gems.md), [ingredients](Skyrim_Ingredients.md), [books](Skyrim_Books.md), [spell tomes](Skyrim_Spell_Tomes.md), a leveled [Conjuration](Skyrim_Conjuration.md) or [Destruction](Skyrim_Destruction.md) [staff](Skyrim_Staves.md), and a small amount of gold. Bandit Plunderers and Marauders carry more gold and have a chance to carry additional lockpicks than lower-level mages.

[^1](#note_Magicka Recovery2)"Magicka Recovery 2" is an ability that increases magicka regeneration by 2%. This perk is available to NPCs only. [^2](#note_Level24) Bandit Marauder mages begin appearing when the player is level 24, rather than level 25 like the other bandit types.
### One-Handed Melee Bandit Chiefs
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/f/f7/SR-npc-Bandit_16.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_16.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_16.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_16.jpg) A Redguard Bandit Chief ready for battle Bandit Chiefs use the same fighting style as other melee bandits, but are a higher level, which means they have more health, more stamina, and more perks. All Bandit Chiefs carry a leveled dagger ([steel](Skyrim_Steel_Dagger.md), [orcish](Skyrim_Orcish_Dagger.md), or [elven](Skyrim_Elven_Dagger.md)) in addition to one of the following weapons:

- **Mace:** [steel mace](Skyrim_Steel_Mace.md), enchanted [iron mace](Skyrim_Iron_Mace.md), [Orcish mace](Skyrim_Orcish_Mace.md), enchanted steel mace, enchanted Orcish mace, [Dwarven mace](Skyrim_Dwarven_Mace.md), enchanted Dwarven mace, [Elven mace](Skyrim_Elven_Mace.md), enchanted Elven mace, [Nordic mace](Skyrim_Nordic_Mace.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>, enchanted Nordic mace [glass mace](Skyrim_Glass_Mace.md), enchanted glass mace, or [ebony mace](Skyrim_Ebony_Mace.md)
- **Sword:** [steel sword](Skyrim_Steel_Sword.md), enchanted [iron sword](Skyrim_Iron_Sword.md), [Orcish sword](Skyrim_Orcish_Sword.md), enchanted steel sword, enchanted Orcish sword, [Dwarven sword](Skyrim_Dwarven_Sword.md), enchanted Dwarven sword, [Elven sword](Skyrim_Elven_Sword.md), enchanted Elven sword, [Nordic sword](Skyrim_Nordic_Sword.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>, enchanted Nordic sword, [glass sword](Skyrim_Glass_Sword.md), enchanted glass sword, or [ebony sword](Skyrim_Ebony_Sword.md)
- **War Axe:** [steel war axe](Skyrim_Steel_War_Axe.md), enchanted [iron war axe](Skyrim_Iron_War_Axe.md), [Orcish war axe](Skyrim_Orcish_War_Axe.md), enchanted steel war axe, enchanted Orcish war axe, [Dwarven war axe](Skyrim_Dwarven_War_Axe.md), enchanted Dwarven war axe, [Elven war axe](Skyrim_Elven_War_Axe.md), enchanted Elven war axe, [Nordic war axe](Skyrim_Nordic_War_Axe.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>, enchanted Nordic war axe, [glass war axe](Skyrim_Glass_War_Axe.md), enchanted glass war axe, or [ebony war axe](Skyrim_Ebony_War_Axe.md)

The enchanted weapons listed above will have either [fire damage](Skyrim_Fire_Damage.md), [frost damage](Skyrim_Frost_Damage.md), [shock damage](Skyrim_Shock_Damage.md), [magicka damage](Skyrim_Magicka_Damage.md), or [stamina damage](Skyrim_Stamina_Damage.md) enchantments. The strength of the enchantment will vary depending on the level of the item.

Bandit Chiefs wear the following leveled heavy armor:

- **Cuirass:** [banded iron armor](Skyrim_Banded_Iron_Armor.md), [iron armor](Skyrim_Iron_Armor.md), [steel armor](Skyrim_Steel_Armor.md), [steel plate armor](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Armor.md), or [Nordic carved armor](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Armor.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Boots:** [iron boots](Skyrim_Iron_Boots.md), [steel cuffed boots](Skyrim_Steel_Cuffed_Boots.md), [steel shin boots](Skyrim_Steel_Shin_Boots.md), [steel plate boots](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Boots.md), or [Nordic carved boots](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Boots.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Gauntlets:** 50% chance of [iron gauntlets](Skyrim_Iron_Gauntlets.md), [steel Nordic gauntlets](Skyrim_Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets.md), [steel Imperial gauntlets](Skyrim_Steel_Imperial_Gauntlets.md), [steel plate gauntlets](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Gauntlets.md), or [Nordic carved gauntlets](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Gauntlets.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Helmet:** 50% chance of [iron helmet](Skyrim_Iron_Helmet.md), [steel helmet](Skyrim_Steel_Helmet.md), [steel horned helmet](Skyrim_Steel_Horned_Helmet.md), [steel plate helmet](Skyrim_Steel_Plate_Helmet.md), or [Nordic carved helmet](Skyrim_Nordic_Carved_Helmet.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>
- **Shield:** [banded iron shield](Skyrim_Banded_Iron_Shield.md), [iron shield](Skyrim_Iron_Shield.md), [steel shield](Skyrim_Steel_Shield.md), [dwarven shield](Skyrim_Dwarven_Shield.md), [orcish shield](Skyrim_Orcish_Shield.md), [ebony shield](Skyrim_Ebony_Shield.md), or [Nordic shield](Skyrim_Nordic_Shield.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>

In addition to the equipment listed above, all Bandit Chiefs carry a leveled amount of gold.

[^1](#note_Missing Perks) This Bandit Chief is missing the Bone Breaker and Skullcrusher perks. [^2](#note_Two Handed) These Bandit Chiefs have `LItem Bandit Weapon2HBoss` instead of `LItem Bandit Boss Weapon1H`, so they actually carry two-handed weapons. [^3](#note_Less Health) This Bandit Chief has only 282 health instead of 395. [^4](#note_Orcish Dagger) Bandit Chiefs at this level should have an elven dagger, but this one has an orcish dagger.
### Two-Handed Melee Bandit Chiefs
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/b/b6/SR-npc-Bandit_26.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit_26.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_26.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit_26.jpg) A Bandit Chief in steel plate armor, wielding his glass greatsword These Bandit Chiefs wear the same heavy armor as their one-handed allies (without the shield). They carry a leveled dagger ([steel](Skyrim_Steel_Dagger.md), [orcish](Skyrim_Orcish_Dagger.md), or [elven](Skyrim_Elven_Dagger.md)) in addition to one of the following weapons:

- **Battleaxe:** [steel battleaxe](Skyrim_Steel_Battleaxe.md), enchanted [iron battleaxe](Skyrim_Iron_Battleaxe.md), [Orcish battleaxe](Skyrim_Orcish_Battleaxe.md), enchanted steel battleaxe, enchanted Orcish battleaxe, [Dwarven battleaxe](Skyrim_Dwarven_Battleaxe.md), enchanted Dwarven battleaxe, [Elven battleaxe](Skyrim_Elven_Battleaxe.md), enchanted Elven battleaxe, [Nordic battleaxe](Skyrim_Nordic_Battleaxe.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>, enchanted Nordic battleaxe, [glass battleaxe](Skyrim_Glass_Battleaxe.md), enchanted glass battleaxe, or [ebony battleaxe](Skyrim_Ebony_Battleaxe.md)
- **Greatsword:** [steel greatsword](Skyrim_Steel_Greatsword.md), enchanted [iron greatsword](Skyrim_Iron_Greatsword.md), [Orcish greatsword](Skyrim_Orcish_Greatsword.md), enchanted steel greatsword, enchanted Orcish greatsword, [Dwarven greatsword](Skyrim_Dwarven_Greatsword.md), enchanted Dwarven greatsword, [Elven greatsword](Skyrim_Elven_Greatsword.md), enchanted Elven greatsword, [Nordic greatsword](Skyrim_Nordic_Greatsword.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>, enchanted Nordic greatsword, [glass greatsword](Skyrim_Glass_Greatsword.md), enchanted glass greatsword, or [ebony greatsword](Skyrim_Ebony_Greatsword.md)
- **Warhammer:** [steel warhammer](Skyrim_Steel_Warhammer.md), enchanted [iron warhammer](Skyrim_Iron_Warhammer.md), [Orcish warhammer](Skyrim_Orcish_Warhammer.md), enchanted steel warhammer, enchanted Orcish warhammer, [Dwarven warhammer](Skyrim_Dwarven_Warhammer.md), enchanted Dwarven warhammer, [Elven warhammer](Skyrim_Elven_Warhammer.md), enchanted Elven warhammer, [Nordic warhammer](Skyrim_Nordic_Warhammer.md)<sup>[DB](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)</sup>, enchanted Nordic warhammer, [glass warhammer](Skyrim_Glass_Warhammer.md), enchanted glass warhammer, or [ebony warhammer](Skyrim_Ebony_Warhammer.md)

The enchanted weapons listed above will have either [fire damage](Skyrim_Fire_Damage.md), [frost damage](Skyrim_Frost_Damage.md), [shock damage](Skyrim_Shock_Damage.md), [magicka damage](Skyrim_Magicka_Damage.md), or [stamina damage](Skyrim_Stamina_Damage.md) enchantments. The strength of the enchantment will vary depending on the level of the item.

[^1](#note_More Magicka) This Nord bandit chief has a higher [magicka](Skyrim_Magicka.md) value of 40 rather than the standard 25.
### Mistwatch Bandits
[Mistwatch](Skyrim_Mistwatch.md) contains a group of bandits called Mistwatch Bandits; these location-specific bandits can be either [one-handed melee fighters](#One-Handed_Melee), [two-handed melee fighters](#Two-Handed_Melee), [archers](#Archers), or [mages](#Mages), and have the same stats and perks as their ordinary bandit counterparts. They are all members of the [Mistwatch faction](Skyrim_DunMistwatchFaction.md), and will no longer be hostile towards the player should the [Mistwatch](Skyrim_Mistwatch_(quest).md) quest be completed in [Fjola's](Skyrim_Fjola.md) favor.

## Related Quests
Some quests that require going into a bandit hideout or dungeon include:

- **[Infiltration](Skyrim_Infiltration.md)**: Help [Stalleo](Skyrim_Stalleo.md) take back [Treva's Watch](Skyrim_Treva%27s_Watch.md).
- **[Mistwatch](Skyrim_Mistwatch_(quest).md)**: Help [Christer](Skyrim_Christer.md) locate his kidnapped wife [Fjola](Skyrim_Fjola.md).
- **[Silver Lining](Skyrim_Silver_Lining.md)**: Recover a stolen [silver mold](Skyrim_Curious_Silver_Mold.md) for a [silversmith](Skyrim_Endon.md).
- **[Supply and Demand](Skyrim_Supply_and_Demand.md)**: Clear [Cragslane Cavern](Skyrim_Cragslane_Cavern.md) for the [Jarl](Skyrim_Jarl.md) of [Riften](Skyrim_Riften.md).
- **[The Pale Lady](Skyrim_The_Pale_Lady.md)**: Find out what happened in [Frostmere Crypt](Skyrim_Frostmere_Crypt.md).

### [Radiant Quests](Skyrim_Radiant.md#Quest_Locations)
- **[Bounty: Bandit Boss](Skyrim_Bounty__Bandit_Boss.md)**: Eliminate a bandit leader for a bounty reward.
- **[Dungeon Delving](Skyrim_Dungeon_Delving_(Bandits).md)**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a bandit hideout.
- **[Harsh Master](Skyrim_Harsh_Master.md)**: Take care of a runaway crew member.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](Skyrim_Kill_the_Bandit_Leader.md)**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader.
- **[Rescue Mission](Skyrim_Rescue_Mission.md)**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](Skyrim_Companions.md) to rescue a kidnapped citizen.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](Skyrim_Radiant.md#Quest_Locations).

### [World Interactions](Skyrim_World_Interactions.md)
- **[Animals attacking bandit](Skyrim_World_Interactions.md#Animals_attacking_bandit)**

## Dialogue
[![](https://images.uesp.net/thumb/c/c8/SR-npc-Bandit.jpg/200px-SR-npc-Bandit.jpg)](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit.jpg) [](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/File:SR-npc-Bandit.jpg) Bandits gathered around a table If you speak to a bandit who is leaning against a wall, typically guarding the outside of a hideout, they may give a generic, non-hostile response (such as *"You need something?"*), although after a few seconds they will draw their weapon and attack. Male bandits will talk to themselves while idle, but they do not talk to each other unless scripted by a certain location <sup>[*verification needed — verify males only*]</sup>.

### Idling
- *"...retire some day... get myself an island..."*
- *"...never enough gold... just need one good haul..."*
- *"...might pay off my bounty this time... walk into the city a free man..."*
- *"...told him to just hand over the gold, but did he listen? Oh, no... they always have to fight back..."*
- *"...I'll never do another span in that stinking jail... rather die than give myself up..."*
- *"...he he he... two threes? What was he thinking? Fool never saw me pull that ace out of my boot..."*
- *"[Sighing] ...need me some Skooma... the imported stuff... just one last time..."*
- *"...gonna start keepin' a knife in my boot... tired of gettin' disarmed..."*
- *"...should have known she was lying... said she'd wait for me... but they never wait..."*
- *"...lyin' little harlot... that brat ain't mine... could be anyone's... won't get one rusty septim from me..."*
- *"..."go to the college" da said... "use your smarts" he said... like I'm supposed to figure out which college he meant..."*
- *"...hmph, wizards... Now that's power... Bet they got that "secret" magic... can turn wood to gold... yeah... Wish I could turn wood to gold..."*
- *"...mead, mead, mead... kill him to get some beer every now and then? Stupid bees and their stupid honey..."*
- *"...picking pockets, now that's the real art... ...no rough stuff, just take it and go... ...hmph, don't sound like much fun, though..."*
- *"[Singing] ...once was a woman, as fair as an evenin', of springtime in old Stros M'Kai..."*
- *"[Singing] ...with three beers down, the Orc did frown, and bid the Elf goodbye... ...for none could know, 'twas not for show, and someone had to die..."*
- *"...kill 'em, he talks to me again like that... get him when he's sleeping... or poison his meat... see how he likes that."*

### Combat
- *"Never should have come here!"*
- *"Lookee here. Looks like we got ourselves a hero."*
- *"You picked a bad time to get lost, friend."*
- *"Now ain't this a surprise."*
- *"Time to die, hero!"*
- *"Go ahead, try and fight back!"*
- *"Die already so I can take your stuff!"*
- *"Whatcha gonna do? Huh? Whatcha gonna do?"*
- *"Gonna split your belly like an old woman's purse!"*
- *"Gonna rip you... open!"*
- *"You'll be so much easier to rob when you're dead..."*
- *"Tell you what. You start running so I can stab you in the back."*
- *"Can't wait to count out your coin..."*

### Miscellaneous
A male bandit who has just discovered a corpse may say:

- *"What...? Whoever did this, you're dead. You hear me? Dead!"*

When playing as a Khajiit, a bandit may say:

- *"You'll make a fine rug, cat!"*

### Location Specific Dialogue
In Lost Knife Cave, you can hear two bandits having a conversation:

**Bandit #1:** *"So, you're saying you brought that cat down alone?"*

**Bandit #2:** *"Why, you don't think I could do it?"*

**Bandit #1:** *"Wasn't our last catch a cave bear?"*

**Bandit #2:** *"Yeah, why?"*

**Bandit #1:** *"Take down that one with your bare hands too?"*

**Bandit #2:** *"Troll's blood was he a tough one!"*

**Bandit #1:** *"pfft"*

**Bandit #2:** *"But, I've got the key to the Sabre cage. Look!"*

**Bandit #1:** *"What's that supposed to prove? Get back on patrol!"*

## Notes
- Bandits encountered in Skyrim are generally twice as likely to be male than female. In most cases, the leveled lists that spawn bandits list each male bandit twice (except Khajiits) and each female bandit once.
- Most bandits have a [morality](Skyrim_Morality.md) of "Any Crime", which means they're willing to commit any crime. Bandit Chiefs and the "berserker" variety of two-handed fighters, however, have a morality of "No Crime", which means they are unwilling to commit crimes of any sort. Their aggression is the same as any other bandit, though, so they will still attack you on sight.
- Bandits that spawn within the exterior zone of [Treva's Watch](Skyrim_Treva%27s_Watch.md) are set to spawn at a normal leveled list corresponding to your game level. However, bandits which spawn within the interior zone are set to appear 5 levels earlier, which means that at lower levels you will more likely encounter Bandit Marauders, etc.
- There is a bandit imprisoned in [Ravenscar Hollow](Skyrim_Ravenscar_Hollow.md) who has been locked up by [hagravens](Skyrim_Hagraven.md) and will ask you to free him. If he survives the fight with the hagravens, he will demand all of your belongings and you will be forced to kill him. This bandit is one of the few with whom you can exchange more than a couple of lines of conversation.
- [Alternative Armors - Daedric Mail](Skyrim_Alternative_Armors_-_Daedric_Mail.md) [Creation](Skyrim_Creation_Club.md) adds entries for level 48 characters in Bandit Bosses' leveled list, these characters wear [Daedric Mail](Skyrim_Daedric_Mail.md) armor.
- The *[Dragonborn](Skyrim_Dragonborn.md)* add-on makes it possible for high level bandits to appear with [Nordic](Skyrim_Nordic.md) weapons and/or Nordic Carved Armor.
- Version 2.1.0 of the [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch) replaces the [Silver Hand](Skyrim_Silver_Hand.md) members at [Driftshade Refuge](Skyrim_Driftshade_Refuge.md) with regular bandits once the dungeon resets after [Purity of Revenge](Skyrim_Purity_of_Revenge.md) is finished.
- Bandit Chiefs that spawn with a shield will bash you far more often than those who spawn with just a one-handed weapon, or two-handed versions of chiefs. Standard one-handed weapon and shield bandits also do not bash as much as their counterpart bandit chiefs do. It is quite possible to be stun-locked by a bandit chief with a shield, as they bash quickly and very often in quick succession.

## Bugs
- Once the bandits in [Helgen](Skyrim_Helgen.md) arrive, they respawn despite the area being a "no-reset zone". - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.

## See Also
- For dead NPCs named "Bandit", see [Bandit (dead)](Skyrim_Bandit_(dead).md).
- For the bandit enemies added by the [Divine Crusader](Skyrim_Divine_Crusader.md) [Creation](Skyrim_Creation_Club.md), see [Bandit Thief](Skyrim_Bandit_Thief.md).
- For a list of locations where bandits are found, see [this category](https://en.uesp.net/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Places-Bandit_Camps).
- For unmarked bandit camps, see [Unmarked Places](Skyrim_Unmarked_Places.md#Unmarked_Bandit_and_Forsworn_Camps).
